          --monorail-metadata-toggled-bg: var(--monorail-metadata-closed-bg);
        }
        mr-issue-page[codeFont] {
          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;
          align-items: stretch;
          justify-content: flex-start;
          z-index: 200;

          flex-wrap: no-wrap;

        }

        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

            Issue 

1253746

: 

Security: WebAudio oob read in AudioDelayDSPKernel::ProcessKRate


          

<h1>

UserAgent: Mozilla/5.0 (X11; Linux x86_64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) HeadlessChrome/95.0.4628.3 Safari/537.36



<span class="line"><!---->UserAgent: Mozilla/5.0 (X11; Linux x86_64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) HeadlessChrome/95.0.4628.3 Safari/537.36<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





VULNERABILITY DETAILS



<b class="line"><!---->VULNERABILITY DETAILS<!----></b>



<br>





In `AudioDelayDSPKernel::ProcessKRate`, if delay_time is `nan`, the `nan` will be propagated to `read_position`.



<span class="line"><!---->In `AudioDelayDSPKernel::ProcessKRate`, if delay_time is `nan`, the `nan` will be propagated to `read_position`.<!----></span>



<br>





After that `read_position` will be casted to int type and the value will be assigned to `read_index1`. The int value 



<span class="line"><!---->After that `read_position` will be casted to int type and the value will be assigned to `read_index1`. The int value <!----></span>



<br>





converted by nan is very large and definitely exceeds the buffer_length. So `read_pointer` will point to an inaccessible



<span class="line"><!---->converted by nan is very large and definitely exceeds the buffer_length. So `read_pointer` will point to an inaccessible<!----></span>



<br>





memory and the program will crash on memcpy.



<span class="line"><!---->memory and the program will crash on memcpy.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





```c++



<span class="line"><!---->```c++<!----></span>



<br>





void AudioDelayDSPKernel::ProcessKRate(const float* source,



<span class="line"><!---->void AudioDelayDSPKernel::ProcessKRate(const float* source,<!----></span>



<br>





                                       float* destination,



<span class="line"><!---->                                       float* destination,<!----></span>



<br>





                                       uint32_t frames_to_process) {



<span class="line"><!---->                                       uint32_t frames_to_process) {<!----></span>



<br>





  int buffer_length = buffer_.size();



<span class="line"><!---->  int buffer_length = buffer_.size();<!----></span>



<br>





  float* buffer = buffer_.Data();



<span class="line"><!---->  float* buffer = buffer_.Data();<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





  // ...



<span class="line"><!---->  // ...<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





  float sample_rate = SampleRate();



<span class="line"><!---->  float sample_rate = SampleRate();<!----></span>



<br>





  double max_time = MaxDelayTime();



<span class="line"><!---->  double max_time = MaxDelayTime();<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





  // ...



<span class="line"><!---->  // ...<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





  double delay_time = DelayTime(sample_rate);



<span class="line"><!---->  double delay_time = DelayTime(sample_rate);<!----></span>



<br>





  // Make sure the delay time is in a valid range.



<span class="line"><!---->  // Make sure the delay time is in a valid range.<!----></span>



<br>





  delay_time = clampTo(delay_time, 0.0, max_time);



<span class="line"><!---->  delay_time = clampTo(delay_time, 0.0, max_time);<!----></span>



<br>





  double desired_delay_frames = delay_time * sample_rate;



<span class="line"><!---->  double desired_delay_frames = delay_time * sample_rate;<!----></span>



<br>





  int w_index = write_index_;



<span class="line"><!---->  int w_index = write_index_;<!----></span>



<br>





  double read_position = w_index + buffer_length - desired_delay_frames; // <<<<<<<<<< read_position = nan;



<span class="line"><!---->  double read_position = w_index + buffer_length - desired_delay_frames; // &lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt; read_position = nan;<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





  if (read_position >= buffer_length)



<span class="line"><!---->  if (read_position &gt;= buffer_length)<!----></span>



<br>





    read_position -= buffer_length;



<span class="line"><!---->    read_position -= buffer_length;<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





  // Linearly interpolate in-between delay times.  |read_index1| and



<span class="line"><!---->  // Linearly interpolate in-between delay times.  |read_index1| and<!----></span>



<br>





  // |read_index2| are the indices of the frames to be used for



<span class="line"><!---->  // |read_index2| are the indices of the frames to be used for<!----></span>



<br>





  // interpolation.



<span class="line"><!---->  // interpolation.<!----></span>



<br>





  int read_index1 = static_cast<int>(read_position); // <<<<<<<<<< covert nan to a large in value



<span class="line"><!---->  int read_index1 = static_cast&lt;int&gt;(read_position); // &lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt; covert nan to a large in value<!----></span>



<br>





  



<span class="line"><!---->  <!----></span>



<br>





  // ...



<span class="line"><!---->  // ...<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





  // Now copy out the samples from the buffer, starting at the read pointer,



<span class="line"><!---->  // Now copy out the samples from the buffer, starting at the read pointer,<!----></span>



<br>





  // carefully handling wrapping of the read pointer.



<span class="line"><!---->  // carefully handling wrapping of the read pointer.<!----></span>



<br>





  float* read_pointer = &buffer[read_index1]; // <<<<<<<<<< get an invalid pointer



<span class="line"><!---->  float* read_pointer = &amp;buffer[read_index1]; // &lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt; get an invalid pointer<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





  uint32_t remainder = static_cast<uint32_t>(buffer_end - read_pointer);



<span class="line"><!---->  uint32_t remainder = static_cast&lt;uint32_t&gt;(buffer_end - read_pointer);<!----></span>



<br>





  memcpy(sample1, read_pointer, // <<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<<   crash here!!!



<span class="line"><!---->  memcpy(sample1, read_pointer, // &lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;&lt;   crash here!!!<!----></span>



<br>





         sizeof(*sample1) * std::min(frames_to_process, remainder));



<span class="line"><!---->         sizeof(*sample1) * std::min(frames_to_process, remainder));<!----></span>



<br>





  // ...



<span class="line"><!---->  // ...<!----></span>



<br>





```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





VERSION



<b class="line"><!---->VERSION<!----></b>



<br>





Chrome Version: 95.0.4628.3(dev)



<span class="line"><!---->Chrome Version: 95.0.4628.3(dev)<!----></span>



<br>





Operating System: Linux, Windows



<span class="line"><!---->Operating System: Linux, Windows<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





REPRODUCTION CASE



<b class="line"><!---->REPRODUCTION CASE<!----></b>



<br>





1) Build release chromium without dcheck (Chromium 95.0.4628.3 is_debug=false dcheck_always_on=false).



<span class="line"><!---->1) Build release chromium without dcheck (Chromium 95.0.4628.3 is_debug=false dcheck_always_on=false).<!----></span>



<br>





2) Serve crash.html from a server: python3 -m http.server 8605.



<span class="line"><!---->2) Serve crash.html from a server: python3 -m http.server 8605.<!----></span>



<br>





3) Run ./chrome 



<span class="line"><!---->3) Run ./chrome <!----></span>





http://localhost:8605/crash.html

<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.

        /*
         * Really specific class names are necessary because ShadowDOM
         * is disabled for this component.
         */
        .chops-autocomplete-container {
          position: relative;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container table {
          padding: 0;
          font-size: var(--chops-main-font-size);
          color: var(--chops-link-color);
          position: absolute;
          background: var(--chops-white);
          border: var(--chops-accessible-border);
          z-index: 999;
          box-shadow: 2px 3px 8px 0px hsla(0, 0%, 0%, 0.3);
          border-spacing: 0;
          border-collapse: collapse;
          /* In the case when the autocomplete extends the
           * height of the viewport, we want to make sure
           * there's spacing. */
          margin-bottom: 1em;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tbody {
          display: block;
          min-width: 100px;
          max-height: 500px;
          overflow: auto;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr {
          cursor: pointer;
          transition: background 0.2s ease-in-out;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container tr[data-selected] {
          background: var(--chops-active-choice-bg);
          text-decoration: underline;
        }
        .chops-autocomplete-container td {
          padding: 0.25em 8px;
          white-space: nowrap;
        }
        .screenreader-hidden {
          clip: rect(1px, 1px, 1px, 1px);
          height: 1px;
          overflow: hidden;
          position: absolute;
          white-space: nowrap;
          width: 1px;
        }

 window.getTSMonClient().recordIssueDetailSpaTiming();
 });
 </script>

<script type="text/javascript" nonce="">
 runOnLoad(function() {
 if (typeof(ClientLogger) === "function") {
 let cl = new ClientLogger("issues");
 if (cl.started("new-issue")) {
 cl.logEnd("new-issue", null, 120 * 1000);
 }
 if (cl.started("issue-search")) {
 cl.logEnd("issue-search");
 }
 }
 });
</script>
